##### **Controllable Lung Nodule Synthesis via Histogram-Regularized Latent Diffusion Models**
2605.30631v1 by Arunkumar Kannan, Yanbo Zhang, Han Liu, Michael Baumgartner, Jianing Wang, Alexander Hertel, Bogdan Georgescu, Sasa Grbic

While automated diagnosis systems have achieved remarkable success in computed tomography (CT)-based lung cancer screening, their development remains limited by the scarcity of diverse, annotated pulmonary nodule datasets. Diffusion-based generative models offer a promising strategy for data synthesis; however, many existing conditional approaches primarily optimize spatial reconstruction losses, which encourage voxel-wise similarity but may inadequately constrain lesion-level intensity distributions. As a result, these methods may produce over-smoothed texture profiles and underrepresent the distinct attenuation characteristics of different nodule subtypes, including solid, part-solid, and ground-glass nodules. To address this challenge, we propose a controllable latent diffusion model that synthesizes pulmonary nodules within full 3D CT volumes while accurately modeling nodule-specific intensity distributions. Specifically, rather than relying solely on spatial losses, we introduce a histogram-based regularization term that constrains voxel intensity distributions during the generative process. The model combines subtype, spatial mask, and Hounsfield unit (HU) histogram conditioning with the differentiable feature-space histogram regularization term to better align lesion-level intensity distributions, improving the visual plausibility and subtype consistency of synthesized nodules. Extensive experiments on lung CT data demonstrate that our framework achieves strong visual realism, validated through both quantitative metrics and a visual Turing test. Furthermore, when used for data augmentation, the generated nodules improve performance in downstream clinical tasks, particularly for underrepresented nodule subtypes, and show a potential benefit for subtype-informed malignancy classification.

摘要：雖然自動診斷系統在基於計算機斷層掃描 (CT) 的肺癌篩檢中取得了顯著成功，但其發展仍受到多樣化、標註的肺結節數據集稀缺的限制。基於擴散的生成模型提供了一種有前景的數據合成策略；然而，許多現有的條件方法主要優化空間重建損失，這鼓勵體素級的相似性，但可能不足以約束病變級別的強度分佈。因此，這些方法可能會產生過於平滑的紋理特徵，並且未能充分代表不同結節亞型的獨特衰減特徵，包括實性、部分實性和磨玻璃結節。為了解決這一挑戰，我們提出了一種可控的潛在擴散模型，該模型在完整的 3D CT 體積內合成肺結節，同時準確建模結節特定的強度分佈。具體而言，我們不僅依賴空間損失，還引入了一個基於直方圖的正則化項，在生成過程中約束體素強度分佈。該模型結合了亞型、空間掩膜和亨斯菲爾德單位 (HU) 直方圖條件，與可微分的特徵空間直方圖正則化項一起，更好地對齊病變級別的強度分佈，提高了合成結節的視覺真實性和亞型一致性。在肺 CT 數據上的大量實驗表明，我們的框架實現了強大的視覺真實性，通過定量指標和視覺圖靈測試進行驗證。此外，當用於數據增強時，生成的結節提高了下游臨床任務的性能，特別是對於代表性不足的結節亞型，並顯示出對亞型知情的惡性分類的潛在益處。

##### **The Architecture of Errors: From Universal Impossibility to Patch-Local LLM Reliability**
2605.30628v1 by Mikhail L. Arbuzov, Lee Mosbacker, Sisong Bei, Ziwei Dong, Dmitri Kalaev, Alexey Shvets

Universal LLM reliability is not a finite-library problem: across all possible tasks, tools, schemas, knowledge sources, and evaluator expectations, new intervention-distinguishable failure modes can appear without bound, so no finite intervention dictionary can guarantee bounded residual error for every such mode. But deployed systems do not operate over the whole universe. They operate inside operationally bounded patches (legal review, medical RAG, code repair, customer-support agents, contract extraction) with recurring tasks, schemas, tools, and evaluator expectations. Within such patches, empirical evidence suggests failures are sparse, repetitive, and concentrated in a small recurring catalogue, so reliability becomes a local catalogue-discovery and intervention-coverage problem rather than an exponential token-length problem. We formalize this transition with two propositions and one corollary. Proposition 1 is the worst-case-mode-wise negative result: no finite intervention dictionary covers every distinguishable failure mode of an unbounded domain. Corollary 1 is the inverse-discovery implication: the logarithmic upper bound on mode discovery cannot accommodate linearly more distinct tail modes without exponentially more observed hard-failure events. Proposition 2 is the positive patch-local result: under log active-mode exposure and head-heavy coverage, a sufficient per-hard-decision intervention budget grows polylogarithmically in sequence length and becomes domain-constant once the patch catalogue saturates. The framework relocates rather than dissolves long-context difficulty: where the number of hard decisions itself grows with task length, reliability remains hard; the contribution is to identify the on-axis intervention rather than to make those regimes easy.

摘要：普遍的 LLM 可靠性並不是一個有限庫問題：在所有可能的任務、工具、架構、知識來源和評估者期望中，新的干預可區分失敗模式可以無限出現，因此沒有任何有限的干預字典可以保證每一種模式的有界殘差誤差。但已部署的系統並不在整個宇宙中運作。它們在操作上有限的區域內運作（法律審查、醫療 RAG、代碼修復、客戶支持代理、合同提取），這些區域具有重複的任務、架構、工具和評估者期望。在這些區域內，經驗證據表明失敗是稀疏的、重複的，並集中在一個小的重複目錄中，因此可靠性成為一個局部目錄發現和干預覆蓋問題，而不是一個指數令牌長度問題。我們用兩個命題和一個推論來形式化這一過渡。命題 1 是最壞情況模式的負結果：沒有任何有限的干預字典可以涵蓋無界域的每一個可區分失敗模式。推論 1 是反向發現的含義：模式發現的對數上限無法容納線性增長的不同尾部模式，而不需要指數增長的觀察到的硬失敗事件。命題 2 是正面的區域本地結果：在對數主動模式暴露和頭重覆蓋下，每個硬決策的干預預算隨序列長度以多對數方式增長，並且一旦區域目錄飽和，就變得與領域常數相關。該框架重新定位而不是解決長上下文的困難：當硬決策的數量隨著任務長度增長時，可靠性仍然很難；貢獻在於識別軸心干預，而不是使這些範疇變得容易。

##### **Scientific Machine Learning for Engine Health Management and Remaining Useful Life Prediction**
2605.30593v1 by Jostein Barry-Straume, Changmin Son, Adrian Sandu, Gavan Burke, Rekha Sundararajan, Andrew Rimell, James G. Steinrock

Engine Health Management (EHM) depends on reliable forecasting of Remaining Useful Life (RUL) and on tracking thermal indicators such as turbine gas temperature (TGT). In practice, real-world fleet data are heterogeneous and non-stationary, and point predictions alone are insufficient for risk-aware maintenance decisions. This paper presents a multi-task scientific machine learning framework for turbine prognostics that jointly predicts turbine gas temperature untrimmed (TGTU), Delta Turbine Gas Temperature (DTGT), and RUL, with quantified uncertainty in the form of prediction intervals whose empirical coverage is evaluated. A shared sequence encoder (convolutional front-end with residual bidirectional LSTM layers and attention pooling) feeds task-specific heads, including mean--variance estimation for probabilistic regression and, optionally, a survival head for threshold-based event modeling. The framework is designed to be tunable via a small set of practitioner-facing parameters (e.g., DTGT thresholding rules and RUL target construction) so that deployment can align with in-house policies and proprietary criteria. The predictive performance of the proposed framework is evaluated using both point and interval metrics, including mean absolute error (MAE), prediction interval coverage probability (PICP), mean prediction interval width (MPIW), and the coverage--width criterion (CWC). Results are reported both in aggregate and stratified by flight phase and maintenance segment to highlight operational-context effects and to support uncertainty-aware monitoring.

摘要：引擎健康管理（EHM）依賴於對剩餘使用壽命（RUL）的可靠預測，以及對熱指標如渦輪氣體溫度（TGT）的追蹤。實際上，現實世界的艦隊數據是異質的且非平穩的，僅有的點預測不足以支持風險意識的維護決策。本文提出了一個多任務科學機器學習框架，用於渦輪預測，該框架共同預測未修整的渦輪氣體溫度（TGTU）、渦輪氣體溫度變化（DTGT）和RUL，並以預測區間的形式量化不確定性，評估其經驗覆蓋率。共享序列編碼器（帶有殘差雙向LSTM層和注意力池化的卷積前端）為任務特定的頭部提供數據，包括用於概率回歸的均值-方差估計，並可選擇性地提供基於閾值的事件建模的生存頭。該框架旨在通過一小組面向實踐者的參數（例如，DTGT閾值規則和RUL目標構建）進行調整，以便部署能夠與內部政策和專有標準對齊。所提出框架的預測性能使用點和區間指標進行評估，包括平均絕對誤差（MAE）、預測區間覆蓋概率（PICP）、平均預測區間寬度（MPIW）和覆蓋-寬度標準（CWC）。結果以總體和按飛行階段及維護段進行分層報告，以突顯操作上下文的影響並支持不確定性意識的監控。

##### **Counterfactual Evaluation Reveals Hidden Capability Profiles in Clinical LLMs and Agents**
2605.30590v1 by Matt Turk

Two clinical AI systems can score nearly identically on coverage-based rubrics yet behave radically differently when their patient inputs change: one updates its recommendations to match the new clinical signal, while the other produces the same output regardless. We introduce the Causal Sensitivity Score (CSS), a pre-registered interventional metric that mutates oncology tumor-board cases along five clinically meaningful dimensions - biomarker flips, prior-treatment failures, biomarker removals, surgery-status changes, and stage perturbations - and scores whether each model updates its recommendations in the pre-registered correct direction using a {0, 0.5, 1.0} scale. Benchmarked against the Consensus Match Score (CMS), a coverage-based weighted recall metric, six frontier models from three labs evaluated in single-shot inference across 224 cases rank in nearly opposite orders: all six models change rank, the CMS-worst model becomes CSS-best, and one upper-mid CMS model ranks last on CSS. We further surface a universal safety blind spot: every frontier model fails on surgery-status interventions (at most 17.2% CSS on Family D), a finding CMS does not expose. The metric also transfers to tool-using agents: in a ReAct-style experiment, tool use improves CSS for five of six models (+2.5 to +20.3 percentage points), yet the lowest-CSS model retrieves the same chart sections and still fails to update its recommendations - revealing a structural responsiveness deficit visible only under counterfactual evaluation. Cross-judge replication and three-rater medical-professional validation confirm the aggregate findings. Interventional pre-registered metrics like CSS complement coverage-based evaluation for clinical AI agents: they capture responsiveness that coverage metrics miss and offer a candidate dense reward signal for future agentic RL systems.

摘要：兩個臨床 AI 系統在基於覆蓋率的評分標準上幾乎得分相同，但當患者輸入變化時，它們的行為卻截然不同：一個系統根據新的臨床信號更新其建議，而另一個系統則無論如何都產生相同的輸出。我們介紹了因果敏感度分數 (CSS)，這是一個預註冊的干預指標，沿著五個臨床意義重大的維度變更腫瘤委員會案例——生物標記翻轉、先前治療失敗、生物標記移除、手術狀態變更和階段擾動——並評分每個模型是否在預註冊的正確方向上更新其建議，使用 {0, 0.5, 1.0} 的標準。與共識匹配分數 (CMS) 進行基準比較，來自三個實驗室的六個前沿模型在 224 個案例中的單次推理評估中幾乎排名相反：所有六個模型的排名都發生變化，CMS 最差的模型成為 CSS 最佳，而一個中上等的 CMS 模型在 CSS 中排名最後。我們進一步揭示了一個普遍的安全盲點：每個前沿模型在手術狀態干預上都失敗（在 D 類家庭中最多 17.2% CSS），這一發現是 CMS 所未揭示的。該指標還可轉移到使用工具的代理：在 ReAct 風格的實驗中，工具使用提高了六個模型中五個的 CSS（+2.5 到 +20.3 個百分點），然而最低 CSS 的模型檢索相同的圖表部分，仍然未能更新其建議——揭示了只有在反事實評估下才能顯現的結構性反應不足。交叉評審重複和三評審醫療專業驗證確認了總體發現。像 CSS 這樣的干預預註冊指標補充了基於覆蓋率的臨床 AI 代理評估：它們捕捉到覆蓋率指標所忽略的反應性，並為未來的代理強化學習系統提供了一個候選的密集獎勵信號。

##### **Benchmarking Machine Learning Uncertainty Quantification Methodologies for Predicting Turbine Gas Temperature Degradation**
2605.30585v1 by Jostein Barry-Straume, Changmin Son, Adrian Sandu, Gavan Burke, Rekha Sundararajan, Andrew Rimell, James G. Steinrock

Effective prognostics and health management of modern engines relies on accurate turbine gas temperature predictions and robust uncertainty quantification to ensure reliability and safety. This paper investigates five major approaches for constructing prediction intervals -- namely the Delta method, Bayesian Monte Carlo Dropout, Bootstrap method, Lower-Upper Bound Estimation, and Mean-Variance Estimation -- as a means of capturing the uncertainty in neural network predictions of turbine gas temperature. Each approach is implemented within a unified experimental framework that employs cross-validation for hyperparameter selection, repeated train-test splits for performance robustness, and multiple metrics to evaluate both the accuracy and tightness of the intervals. In particular, Coverage Probability, Normalized Mean Prediction Interval Width, and the Coverage Width-based Criterion are measured to comprehensively assess each method's reliability and sharpness. Experiments conducted on a representative turbine gas temperature dataset reveal distinct trade-offs among the five methods in terms of interval coverage, width, and stability. These findings provide a practical guide for selecting and tuning prediction interval methods in engine health management and prognostics, ensuring both interpretability and precision in real-world applications.

摘要：有效的現代引擎預測與健康管理依賴於準確的渦輪氣體溫度預測和穩健的不確定性量化，以確保可靠性和安全性。本文探討了構建預測區間的五種主要方法——即 Delta 方法、貝葉斯蒙特卡羅隨機失效、Bootstrap 方法、上下界估計法和均值-方差估計法——作為捕捉神經網絡對渦輪氣體溫度預測不確定性的一種手段。每種方法都在一個統一的實驗框架內實施，該框架使用交叉驗證進行超參數選擇，重複的訓練-測試拆分以提高性能穩健性，並使用多種指標來評估區間的準確性和緊密性。特別地，測量了覆蓋概率、標準化均值預測區間寬度和基於覆蓋寬度的標準，以全面評估每種方法的可靠性和敏銳度。在一個代表性的渦輪氣體溫度數據集上進行的實驗顯示，這五種方法在區間覆蓋、寬度和穩定性方面存在明顯的權衡。這些發現為在引擎健康管理和預測中選擇和調整預測區間方法提供了實用指南，確保在現實應用中既具可解釋性又具精確性。

##### **Generalistic or Specific Embeddings, Which is Better? An Empirical Study on Search for Clinical Coding in Non-English Languages**
2605.30529v1 by David Rey-Blanco, Roberto Cruz

Sentence-embedding models for semantic search are overwhelmingly developed and evaluated on English corpora. When applied to clinical retrieval in other languages -- particularly retrieval of ICD-10-CM / CIE-10 codes -- recall degrades in ways often masked by aggregate benchmarks. We study whether large generative language models can serve as data factories to close this gap. We build a two-stage retriever (bi-encoder followed by cross-encoder reranker), fine-tuned from a Spanish biomedical encoder (PlanTL-GOB-ES/bsc-bio-ehr-es) on Gemini-generated synthetic data covering English, Spanish, Catalan, Italian, Portuguese and French, and evaluate against BioBERT-ST and the un-tuned Spanish encoder. The bi-encoder alone matches BioBERT-ST on MRR (0.876 vs. 0.866) and overtakes it on R@3 (0.650 vs. 0.626) and R@5 (0.804 vs. 0.790) without English biomedical pretraining. Adding a cross-encoder reranker lifts aggregate R@5 to 0.822 and dominates on four of five languages (+0.017 Spanish, +0.033 Catalan, +0.018 French, +0.037 Portuguese) at the cost of a small English regression. The trade-off is clinically acceptable: Portuguese reaches R@5 = 0.829 vs. BioBERT-ST's 0.714. Contributions: an open recipe for building domain-specific medical retrievers from LLM-generated data; quantification of the learning gain (MRR 0.755 to 0.876, +15.9% with ~19,500 synthetic pairs); and a characterisation of where gains concentrate by language and rank.

摘要：語義搜索的句子嵌入模型主要在英語語料庫上開發和評估。當應用於其他語言的臨床檢索時——特別是ICD-10-CM / CIE-10代碼的檢索——召回率以往往被總體基準掩蓋的方式下降。我們研究大型生成語言模型是否可以作為數據工廠來縮小這一差距。我們構建了一個兩階段檢索器（雙編碼器後接交叉編碼器重排序），從西班牙生物醫學編碼器（PlanTL-GOB-ES/bsc-bio-ehr-es）進行微調，使用涵蓋英語、西班牙語、加泰羅尼亞語、意大利語、葡萄牙語和法語的Gemini生成的合成數據，並與BioBERT-ST和未經微調的西班牙編碼器進行評估。僅雙編碼器在MRR上與BioBERT-ST相匹配（0.876對0.866），並在R@3（0.650對0.626）和R@5（0.804對0.790）上超越它，且不需要英語生物醫學的預訓練。添加交叉編碼器重排序將總體R@5提升至0.822，並在五種語言中的四種語言上佔據主導地位（西班牙語+0.017，加泰羅尼亞語+0.033，法語+0.018，葡萄牙語+0.037），代價是小幅的英語回落。這一權衡在臨床上是可接受的：葡萄牙語的R@5達到0.829，而BioBERT-ST為0.714。貢獻：一個開放的配方，用於從LLM生成的數據構建特定領域的醫療檢索器；學習增益的量化（MRR從0.755提升至0.876，增長15.9%，約19,500對合成數據）；以及對增益集中在哪些語言和排名的特徵描述。

##### **idSCD: Identifying Training Datasets through Semantic Correlation Descriptors**
2605.30462v1 by Andrada Gobeaja, Ionut Hodoroaga, Elena Burceanu, Marius Leordeanu

Can a dataset be recognized from the spurious correlations it induces during training? We argue that datasets leave dataset-specific traces in a model's learned semantic correlation structure: incidental regularities that are predictive within a dataset, but not causal for the underlying task, can be internalized during training. We use this insight to study dataset-level membership inference, moving beyond existing methods that rely on behavioral or distributional evidence such as confidence scores, losses, margins, generated samples, or query responses. We introduce a white-box semantic fingerprinting approach based on semantic correlation descriptors (SCDs), which capture the semantic correlation structure learned by a model and make it comparable across dataset mixtures. In a controlled leave-one-dataset-out diagnostic, SCDs recover dataset-specific changes and perfectly separate matching from non-matching dataset pairs. We then propose a practical SCD-based membership score that tests whether a target dataset is part of a model's training mixture using only the model's SCD and the target dataset's standalone SCD, without requiring leave-one-dataset-out models. Across three diverse experimental settings, with dataset groups for natural language inference, emotion classification, and medical text classification, we test both the advantages and limitations of SCD-based membership inference with different degrees of semantic separation and keyword support between dataset splits. On average, the classifier based on this score achieves the highest performance and the lowest std, outperforming black-box baselines RMIA, Attack-P, and LiRA, as well as the white-box SIF baseline. These results show that dataset membership can be traced through internal semantic correlations, with the largest relative gain exceeding 60% in ROC-AUC when dataset groups expose distinct semantic particularities.

摘要：一個數據集能否從其在訓練過程中引發的虛假相關性中被識別出來？我們認為數據集在模型學習的語義相關結構中留下了特定於數據集的痕跡：在數據集中具有預測性的偶然規律，但對於基礎任務並不具因果關係，可以在訓練過程中內化。我們利用這一見解來研究數據集層級的成員推斷，超越依賴行為或分佈證據（如置信度分數、損失、邊際、生成樣本或查詢響應）的現有方法。我們引入了一種基於語義相關描述符（SCDs）的白盒語義指紋識別方法，該方法捕捉模型學習的語義相關結構，並使其在數據集混合中可比較。在一個受控的留一數據集診斷中，SCDs恢復了特定於數據集的變化，並完美地將匹配和不匹配的數據集對分開。我們接著提出了一種實用的基於SCD的成員分數，該分數僅使用模型的SCD和目標數據集的獨立SCD，測試目標數據集是否是模型訓練混合的一部分，而無需留一數據集模型。在三個不同的實驗設置中，針對自然語言推理、情感分類和醫學文本分類的數據集組，我們測試了基於SCD的成員推斷的優勢和局限性，並考察了數據集拆分之間的語義分離和關鍵字支持的不同程度。平均而言，基於此分數的分類器達到了最高的性能和最低的標準差，超越了黑盒基準RMIA、Attack-P和LiRA，以及白盒SIF基準。這些結果表明，數據集成員可以通過內部語義相關性追蹤，當數據集組暴露出明顯的語義特點時，最大的相對增益超過60%在ROC-AUC中。

##### **MedCase-Structured: A Text-to-FHIR Dataset for Benchmarking Diagnostic Reasoning in Clinically Realistic EHR Settings**
2605.30295v1 by Valentina Bui Muti, Eugénie Dulout, Ziquan Fu

Large language models (LLMs) show promise for clinical reasoning and decision support, but evaluation in realistic, electronic health record-congruent settings remains limited. Existing benchmarks often rely on static datasets or unstructured inputs that do not reflect the structured, interoperable data formats used in clinical systems. We introduce a pipeline for generating clinically realistic HL7 FHIR R4 bundles from unstructured text, enabling controllable evaluation of clinical decision support systems. The pipeline combines staged LLM generation with terminology-grounded validation and repair to reduce hallucinated codes and enforce structural and semantic consistency. Applying this approach to MedCaseReasoning, we construct MedCase-Structured, a synthetic dataset aligned with clinician-authored diagnostic cases, achieving valid FHIR generation for 82.5% of cases. Evaluation on MedCase-Structured reveals consistently lower diagnostic accuracy for LLMs on structured FHIR inputs than with plain text, highlighting the importance of deployment-aligned benchmarking.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在臨床推理和決策支持方面顯示出潛力，但在現實的電子健康記錄相符環境中的評估仍然有限。現有的基準通常依賴於靜態數據集或不結構化的輸入，這些並不反映臨床系統中使用的結構化、可互操作的數據格式。我們介紹了一個從不結構化文本生成臨床現實的HL7 FHIR R4捆綁包的流程，使臨床決策支持系統的可控評估成為可能。該流程結合了分階段的LLM生成與基於術語的驗證和修復，以減少幻覺代碼並強制執行結構和語義的一致性。將這種方法應用於MedCaseReasoning，我們構建了MedCase-Structured，這是一個與臨床醫生撰寫的診斷案例對齊的合成數據集，實現了82.5%案例的有效FHIR生成。在MedCase-Structured上的評估顯示，LLMs在結構化FHIR輸入上的診斷準確性始終低於純文本，突顯了與部署對齊的基準測試的重要性。

##### **LLUMI: Improving LLM Writing Assistance for Mental Health Support with Online Community Feedback**
2605.30273v1 by Jiwon Kim, Maya Ajit, Sherry Gong, Soorya Ram Shimgekar, Dong Whi Yoo, Eshwar Chandrasekharan, Koustuv Saha

Large language models (LLMs) show promise in generating supportive responses for mental health queries, but improving their usefulness, empathy, and safety often requires substantial compute, expert input, and labeled data. At the same time, deploying proprietary, cloud-based models for mental health-related interactions raises important privacy and data-governance concerns, given the sensitivities. To address this challenge, we introduce LLUMI setup that can be hosted in-house within protected environments. LLUMI consists of two complementary components: a generation model (GM), which drafts supportive responses to mental health queries, and an improvement model (IM), which revises an initial human-crafted response. We leverage feedback signals from Reddit mental health communities, using community endorsement patterns such as upvotes and downvotes to construct chosen-rejected response pairs for Supervised Fine Tuning (SFT) and Direct Preference Optimization (DPO). We further align LLUMI using human evaluation across five dimensions: readability, empathy, connection, actionability, and safety. Our results show that, despite relying on smaller open-source models rather than proprietary cloud-based GPT models, LLUMI achieves comparable performance across linguistic analyses and human evaluations. These findings suggest that open-source models, when trained with community-derived preference signals, can support high-quality mental health support assistance while offering a more privacy-preserving alternative for sensitive support contexts.

摘要：大型語言模型（LLMs）在生成支持性回應以應對心理健康問題方面顯示出潛力，但提高其有用性、同理心和安全性通常需要大量的計算資源、專家意見和標記數據。<lb/>同時，對於心理健康相關互動部署專有的雲端模型會引發重要的隱私和數據治理問題，考慮到其敏感性。<lb/>為了解決這一挑戰，我們介紹了LLUMI設置，該設置可以在受保護的環境中內部托管。<lb/>LLUMI由兩個互補組件組成：生成模型（GM），負責草擬對心理健康問題的支持性回應，以及改進模型（IM），負責修訂最初的人類創建的回應。<lb/>我們利用來自Reddit心理健康社區的反饋信號，使用社區認可模式，例如贊成票和反對票，來構建選擇-拒絕的回應對，以進行監督式微調（SFT）和直接偏好優化（DPO）。<lb/>我們進一步通過五個維度進行人類評估來對齊LLUMI：可讀性、同理心、連結性、可行性和安全性。<lb/>我們的結果顯示，儘管依賴於較小的開源模型而非專有的雲端GPT模型，LLUMI在語言分析和人類評估方面達到了可比的表現。<lb/>這些發現表明，當使用社區衍生的偏好信號進行訓練時，開源模型可以支持高質量的心理健康支持協助，同時為敏感支持情境提供更具隱私保護的替代方案。

##### **Evolving Features vs Evolving Entire Trees with GP for Interpretable Survival Analysis**
2605.30119v1 by Thalea Schlender, Peter A. N. Bosman, Tanja Alderliesten

Survival analysis concerns the task of predicting the time until an event occurs. Often used in the medical field, survival analysis deals with incomplete (i.e., censored) data, for instance, from patients who did not experience the event during the duration of the study. For practical use, both accuracy and interpretability are important.
  Survival trees are easy-to-follow survival models that split the patient cohort recursively into discrete patient groups. Whilst survival trees can capture complex relationships, they typically need to grow large, threatening interpretability. Moreover, survival trees are often built using greedy approaches that may overlook globally optimal split combinations, limiting predictive performance.
  Shallow survival trees require expressive, higher-order feature combinations to achieve competitive accuracy. We therefore use genetic programming to multi-objectively evolve inherently inspectable feature sets and study how they interact with different tree induction strategies. We further introduce an evolutionary approach that jointly optimises the survival tree structure and the non-linear split logic.
  Our findings demonstrate that evolutionary feature construction improves predictive performance across different tree induction strategies on two real-world datasets and two different survival tree depths. Full joint evolution has the overall highest potential to propose multiple inherently inspectable shallow survival trees of good performance.

摘要：生存分析關注預測事件發生的時間。生存分析常用於醫學領域，處理不完整（即被刪減的）數據，例如來自在研究期間未經歷事件的患者。對於實際應用來說，準確性和可解釋性都是重要的。<lb/>
生存樹是易於理解的生存模型，將患者群體遞歸地劃分為離散的患者組。雖然生存樹可以捕捉複雜的關係，但它們通常需要增長到較大，這會威脅到可解釋性。此外，生存樹通常是使用貪婪的方法構建的，這可能會忽略全局最優的劃分組合，限制預測性能。<lb/>
淺層生存樹需要表達性強的高階特徵組合才能達到競爭性的準確性。因此，我們使用遺傳編程來多目標進化固有可檢查的特徵集，並研究它們如何與不同的樹引導策略互動。我們進一步引入一種進化方法，聯合優化生存樹的結構和非線性劃分邏輯。<lb/>
我們的研究結果顯示，進化特徵構建提高了在兩個真實世界數據集和兩種不同生存樹深度下不同樹引導策略的預測性能。完全聯合進化具有提出多個固有可檢查的淺層生存樹的最佳潛力，且其性能良好。

##### **Domain-Specific Data Synthesis for LLMs via Minimal Sufficient Representation Learning**
2605.30039v2 by Tong Ye, Hang Yu, Tengfei Ma, Xuhong Zhang, Jianguo Li, Peng Di, Peiyu Liu, Jianwei Yin, Wenhai Wang

Large Language Models have demonstrated remarkable progress in general-purpose capabilities and can achieve strong performance in specific domains through fine-tuning on domain-specific data. However, acquiring high-quality data for target domains remains a significant challenge. Existing data synthesis approaches follow a deductive paradigm, heavily relying on explicit domain descriptions expressed in natural language and careful prompt engineering, limiting their applicability in real-world scenarios where domains are difficult to describe or formally articulate. In this work, we tackle the underexplored problem of domain-specific data synthesis through an inductive paradigm, where the target domain is defined only through a set of reference examples, particularly when domain characteristics are difficult to articulate in natural language. We propose a novel framework, DOMINO, that learns a minimal sufficient domain representation from reference samples and leverages it to guide the generation of domain-aligned synthetic data. DOMINO integrates prompt tuning with a contrastive disentanglement objective to separate domain-level patterns from sample-specific noise, mitigating overfitting while preserving core domain characteristics. Theoretically, we prove that DOMINO expands the support of the synthetic data distribution, ensuring greater diversity. Empirically, on challenging coding benchmarks where domain definitions are implicit, fine-tuning on data synthesized by DOMINO improves Pass@1 accuracy by up to 4.63\% over strong, instruction-tuned backbones, demonstrating its effectiveness and robustness. This work establishes a new paradigm for domain-specific data synthesis, enabling practical and scalable domain adaptation without manual prompt design or natural language domain specifications.

摘要：大型語言模型在通用能力上展現了顯著的進步，並且能夠通過對特定領域數據的微調在特定領域中達到強勁的表現。<lb/>然而，獲取目標領域的高質量數據仍然是一個重大挑戰。<lb/>現有的數據合成方法遵循演繹範式，主要依賴於用自然語言表達的明確領域描述和仔細的提示工程，這限制了它們在現實場景中的適用性，尤其是在領域難以描述或正式表達的情況下。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們著手解決通過歸納範式進行特定領域數據合成的未被充分探索的問題，目標領域僅通過一組參考示例來定義，特別是在領域特徵難以用自然語言表達的情況下。<lb/>我們提出了一個新框架，DOMINO，該框架從參考樣本中學習最小充分的領域表示，並利用它來指導生成與領域對齊的合成數據。<lb/>DOMINO將提示調整與對比解耦目標相結合，以將領域級模式與樣本特定噪聲分離，減輕過擬合的同時保留核心領域特徵。<lb/>理論上，我們證明了DOMINO擴展了合成數據分佈的支持，確保了更大的多樣性。<lb/>在挑戰性的編碼基準上，當領域定義是隱含的時候，對DOMINO合成的數據進行微調使Pass@1準確率提高了最多4.63\%，超過了強大的指令調整骨幹，顯示了其有效性和穩健性。<lb/>這項工作建立了一個新的特定領域數據合成範式，使得在沒有手動提示設計或自然語言領域規範的情況下實現實用和可擴展的領域適應成為可能。

##### **Genetically Aligned Patient Representations Improve Hematological Diagnosis**
2605.29980v1 by Muhammed Furkan Dasdelen, Fatih Ozlugedik, Ilaria Looser, Rao Muhammad Umer, Christian Pohlkamp, Carsten Marr

Multimodal alignment of histopathology encoders with transcriptomic and genomic data has been shown to significantly improve performance in downstream diagnostic tasks. Hematological cytology is unique in that visual single-cell evaluation is often paired with cytogenetics and molecular genetics for blood cancer diagnosis. In this study, we present a framework to align single white blood cell images with chromosomal aberrations (karyotype) and somatic mutations from targeted gene panels. Our training strategy follows a two-stage approach: (i) self-supervised, vision-only pretraining of a transformer aggregator using an iBOT head on a cohort of over 1500 patients, and (ii) genetic alignment via supervised contrastive loss on acute myeloid leukemia patients. Our genetically aligned patient encoder improves hematological diagnostic tasks, outperforming slide-level histopathology foundation models. Additionally, the model provides off-the-shelf retrieval capabilities for diseases and genetic alterations. Incorporating genetic data into patient encoders increases the quality of patient representations, providing a framework that aligns with clinical diagnostic workflows and paves the way for future multimodal hematology-specific AI. The code and model weights are available at https://github.com/marrlab/GenBloom.

摘要：多模態對齊組織病理學編碼器與轉錄組和基因組數據的研究顯示，在下游診斷任務中顯著提高了性能。血液學細胞學的獨特之處在於，視覺單細胞評估通常與細胞遺傳學和分子遺傳學相結合，用於血癌診斷。在這項研究中，我們提出了一個框架，將單個白血球圖像與染色體異常（核型）和來自靶向基因面板的體細胞突變對齊。我們的訓練策略遵循兩階段方法：（i）對超過1500名患者的Transformer聚合器進行自我監督的僅視覺預訓練，使用iBOT頭，和（ii）通過對急性骨髓性白血病患者的監督對比損失進行基因對齊。我們的基因對齊患者編碼器改善了血液學診斷任務，超越了幻燈片級別的組織病理學基礎模型。此外，該模型提供了現成的疾病和基因變異檢索能力。將基因數據納入患者編碼器提高了患者表示的質量，提供了一個與臨床診斷工作流程對齊的框架，為未來的多模態血液學特定AI鋪平了道路。代碼和模型權重可在 https://github.com/marrlab/GenBloom 獲得。

##### **Internal Representation, Not Clinical Knowledge: Where Apparent LLM Triage Failures Originate**
2605.29889v1 by David Fraile Navarro, Berardino Como, Jialei Sheng, Soundariya Ananthan, Shlomo Berkovsky

Patient-voiced clinical-triage benchmarks report high under-triage rates for consumer LLMs for constrained multiple-choice output, yet the same cases score differently with free-text. We ask whether output format changes the model's \emph{clinical representation} or only the mapping from a preserved representation to an answer. Using sparse-autoencoder (SAE) features in Gemma 3 4B/12B IT and Qwen3-8B, we find the same medical features fire on the shared clinical narrative under both formats but go {silent} at the multiple-choice decision token in all the cases at every model. Three independent methods (natural-language autoencoder verbalization, decision-token logit attribution, and top-feature characterization) agree that scaffold and format features, but not medical features, drive the decision logits. Behaviorally, the multiple-choice penalty inverts under both structured and natural-language input, option-order shuffle rules out positional bias, and the gap is dominated by off-by-one decision (the model picks an adjacent acuity letter to the gold answer) rather than knowledge failure. Thus, the failure originates in the output format and not in the clinical representation.

摘要：病人聲音的臨床分流基準報告顯示，消費者 LLM 在受限的多選輸出中存在高比例的低分流率，但在自由文本中相同的案例得分卻不同。我們詢問輸出格式是否改變了模型的 \emph{臨床表徵}，還是僅僅改變了從保留的表徵到答案的映射。使用 Gemma 3 4B/12B IT 和 Qwen3-8B 中的稀疏自編碼器 (SAE) 特徵，我們發現相同的醫療特徵在兩種格式下的共享臨床敘事中都會被激活，但在所有模型的多選決策標記中卻保持 {靜默}。三種獨立的方法（自然語言自編碼器口頭化、決策標記邏輯歸因和頂部特徵特徵化）一致認為，支架和格式特徵，而不是醫療特徵，驅動了決策邏輯。行為上，多選懲罰在結構化和自然語言輸入下都會反轉，選項順序隨機打亂排除了位置偏見，而這一差距主要由錯誤一個的決策主導（模型選擇與金標答案相鄰的敏感度字母），而不是知識失敗。因此，失敗源於輸出格式，而不是臨床表徵。

##### **CardioLens: Revealing the Clinical Reality Gap of MLLMs via Multi-Sequence Cardiac MRI Evaluations**
2606.00123v1 by Zixian Su, Hongkai Zhang, Fan Gao, Encheng Su, Taiping Qu, Jingwei Guo, Nan Zhang, Hui Wang, Zhen Zhou, Kairui Bo, Yan Chen, Yue Ren, Shuai Li, Lei Xu, Henggui Zhang

Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have shown strong performance on public medical benchmarks, yet existing evaluations often remain weak proxies for clinical use, relying on isolated inputs and simplified recognition-style tasks. We introduce CardioLens, a leakage-resistant evaluation testbed for multi-sequence Cardiovascular Magnetic Resonance (CMR), constructed from private hospital archives through a rigorous report-to-QA construction and verification pipeline. CardioLens contains 473,896 slices and 13,494 verified QA pairs across 4D Cine, LGE, perfusion, and T2-weighted imaging, and evaluates three stages of CMR interpretation: image understanding, report generation, and disease diagnosis. Across 24 state-of-the-art MLLMs, CardioLens reveals a substantial clinical reality gap: models perform poorly overall, with performance degrading along the real CMR workflow. Confusion analysis further shows a category-collapse failure mode, where models default to frequent abnormal categories rather than distinguishing clinically distinct findings. To rule out MLLM-compatible input construction as the primary cause, we compare random, clinically motivated, and data-driven slice selection protocols under different slice budgets; performance changes only marginally, typically by about 1%. Explicit reasoning prompts also fail to rescue performance, often making models more conservative rather than improving visual evidence use. These results show that current MLLMs remain far from reliable CMR interpretation, where clinical decisions require integrating distributed evidence across sequences, views, and temporal phases. CardioLens provides a clinically grounded testbed for developing next-generation MLLMs toward real-world clinical deployment.

摘要：多模態大型語言模型（MLLMs）在公共醫療基準上表現出色，但現有的評估往往仍然是臨床使用的弱代理，依賴孤立的輸入和簡化的識別風格任務。我們介紹了CardioLens，一個抗洩漏的多序列心血管磁共振（CMR）評估測試平台，該平台通過嚴格的報告到質量保證的建構和驗證流程，從私人醫院檔案中構建而成。CardioLens包含473,896個切片和13,494對經過驗證的質量保證對，涵蓋4D Cine、LGE、灌注和T2加權影像，並評估CMR解釋的三個階段：影像理解、報告生成和疾病診斷。在24個最先進的MLLMs中，CardioLens顯示出顯著的臨床現實差距：模型整體表現不佳，隨著真實CMR工作流程的推進，性能下降。混淆分析進一步顯示了一種類別崩潰的失敗模式，模型傾向於默認頻繁的異常類別，而不是區分臨床上不同的發現。為了排除與MLLM兼容的輸入構建作為主要原因，我們在不同的切片預算下比較隨機、臨床驅動和數據驅動的切片選擇協議；性能變化僅為邊際，通常約為1%。明確的推理提示也未能挽救性能，往往使模型變得更加保守，而不是改善視覺證據的使用。這些結果表明，當前的MLLMs距離可靠的CMR解釋仍然相去甚遠，臨床決策需要整合跨序列、視圖和時間階段的分散證據。CardioLens提供了一個以臨床為基礎的測試平台，用於開發下一代MLLMs，以實現現實世界的臨床部署。

##### **A unified deeplearning framework for contrast-phase-specific virtual monochromatic imaging**
2605.29753v1 by Antony Jerald, Hemant K Aggarwal, Brian Nett, Avinash Gopal, Phaneendra K Yalavarthy, Bipul Das, Rajesh Langoju

Dual-energy CT (DECT) enables virtual monochromatic imaging (VMI) and improved contrast resolution, but its clinical adoption is limited by hardware complexity and cost. In this work, we propose a unified deep learning framework that synthesizes contrast-phase-specific virtual monochromatic 50 keV images from single-energy CT (SECT) data by leveraging contrast phase information as a prior. The model is trained using DECT-derived 70 keV and 50 keV image pairs across four contrast phases -- Angio, Arterial, Portal, and Delayed -- using a novel prior conditioning architecture that integrates contrast phase priors into the energy transformation process. We demonstrate that the proposed unified model achieves contrast enhancement and generalizes well across contrast phases. Additionally, we show that the model can generate 50 keV-like images from SECT inputs, preserving contrast phase-specific dynamics.

摘要：雙能量 CT (DECT) 使得虛擬單色成像 (VMI) 和改善對比度解析度成為可能，但其臨床應用受到硬體複雜性和成本的限制。<lb/>在這項工作中，我們提出了一個統一的深度學習框架，通過利用對比度相位信息作為先驗，從單能量 CT (SECT) 數據合成對比相位特定的虛擬單色 50 keV 圖像。<lb/>該模型使用來自 DECT 的 70 keV 和 50 keV 圖像對進行訓練，涵蓋四個對比相位 -- 血管相位、動脈相位、門脈相位和延遲相位 -- 使用一種新穎的先驗條件架構，將對比相位先驗整合到能量轉換過程中。<lb/>我們證明了所提出的統一模型實現了對比度增強，並在對比相位之間良好泛化。<lb/>此外，我們顯示該模型可以從 SECT 輸入生成類似 50 keV 的圖像，保持對比相位特定的動態。
